| [Let the user set a default Jira Project](https://feedback.canny.io/feature-requests/p/let-the-user-set-a-default-jira-project)<br>让用户设置默认的 Jira 项目 | When you create a jira issue from Canny, Canny selects the first jira project in the list. Because of the way we filter things in jira, once an issue is placed in the wrong project, it's basically in a black hole. So, a customer gives us great feedback, we feed it into jira so that we can plan the work, and then it suffers a sad and lonely death.<br>Each of our users has a project that they usually work from, so giving the user the ability to set their default project would  prevent this problem from happening so often.<br><br>当您从 Canny 创建 jira 问题时，Canny 会选择列表中的第一个 jira 项目。当我创建一个问题时，我自然会考虑为该问题起一个好名字并很好地描述它......结果，在创建问题时很容易忘记更改项目。由于我们在 jira 中过滤事物的方式，一旦将问题放入错误的项目中，它基本上就陷入了黑洞。因此，客户给了我们很好的反馈，我们将其输入 jira 以便我们可以规划工作，然后它就悲伤而孤独地死去。<br>我们的每个用户都有一个他们通常使用的项目，因此让用户能够设置他们的默认项目可以防止此问题经常发生。 | 8 | 0 |

| [Allow custom types of impact weights (such as .25, .5, 1, 2, and 3 for impact)](https://feedback.canny.io/feature-requests/p/allow-custom-types-of-impact-weights-such-as-25-5-1-2-and-3-for-impact)<br>允许自定义类型的冲击权重（例如冲击权重为 0.25、0.5、1、2 和 3） | It seems like many rubrics for scoring an idea's impact use scales not supported by Canny. For example, I want to mimic the RICE model and be able to score my impact using a common scale of .25, .5, 1, 2, and 3. Five stars is the closest supported measurement in Canny. However, that means that the greatest possible disparity in value is 5 rather than 12. I could use Fibonacci, but then there are too many options (I want a limited number of options).<br><br>Canny 似乎不支持对想法影响力使用量表进行评分的许多标准。例如，我想模仿 RICE 模型，并能够使用 0.25、0.5、1、2 和 3 的通用量表对我的影响进行评分。五颗星是 Canny 中支持的最接近的测量值。然而，这意味着最大可能的价值差异是 5，而不是 12。我可以使用斐波那契，但选项太多（我想要有限数量的选项）。 | 2 | 1 |

| [API & Docs improvement](https://feedback.canny.io/feature-requests/p/api-docs-improvement)<br>API 和文档改进 | Hi, while integrating with the Canny API we noticed some challenges that could be improved. For example, /users/list only returns a subset of users (e.g., tracked users), meaning we have to manually call /users/retrieve for each user to get a complete list, which makes bulk operations slow and complex. Additionally, /votes/create often fails silently without clear JSON error messages. Bulk endpoints for creating users and casting votes would make batch operations much easier. It would also help to support authentication via HTTP headers (Bearer tokens) instead of including API keys in the payload, and to provide clearer documentation with end-to-end examples (e.g., creating users with tags and casting timestamped votes on their behalf).<br><br>您好，在与 Canny API 集成时，我们注意到一些可以改进的挑战。例如， /users/list 只返回用户的子集（例如，跟踪的用户），这意味着我们必须为每个用户手动调用 /users/retrieve 才能获得完整的列表，这使得批量操作变得缓慢而复杂。此外，/votes/create 经常会默默地失败，并且没有明确的 JSON 错误消息。用于创建用户和投票的批量端点将使批量操作变得更加容易。它还将有助于支持通过 HTTP 标头（承载令牌）进行身份验证，而不是在有效负载中包含 API 密钥，并提供更清晰的文档和端到端示例（例如，使用标签创建用户并代表他们进行带时间戳的投票）。 | 1 | 0 |

| [Unify admin & public views to improve usability](https://feedback.canny.io/feature-requests/p/unify-admin-public-views-to-improve-usability)<br>统一管理员和公众视图以提高可用性 | I find it really hard to navigate between the admin and public views because there are two different layouts for each view. What often happen is that;<br>1. I go to our public roadmap via eduflow.canny.io.<br>2. I see a notification for a new feature request and click it.<br>3. I want to change the status or board.<br>4. I change to the admin view to do so.<br>5. The layout changes completely leaving me confused. Everything has changed position. The board name is no longer a dropdown in the top navigation, but a dropdown in a side menu. The status is no longer written below the heading, but is a dropdown in a side menu. The voters section have moved from the left side to the bottom right. I now have three columns instead of two. The header is suddenly full width with different menu items and a different color.<br>6. I make my changes and want to go back to see the roadmap view. The roadmap view now also looks different, because I'm in the admin view.<br>I think it would improve usability dramatically if the two views merged into one. This might be a tough design challenge to crack, but one that I think would have a huge impact for admins.<br><br>我发现在管理视图和公共视图之间导航真的很困难，因为每个视图都有两种不同的布局。经常发生的情况是；<br>1. 我通过 eduflow.canny.io 访问我们的公共路线图。<br>2. 我看到新功能请求的通知并单击它。<br>3. 我想更改状态或面板。<br>4. 我切换到管理视图来执行此操作。<br>5. 布局完全改变，让我很困惑。一切都改变了位置。板名称不再是顶部导航中的下拉菜单，而是侧面菜单中的下拉菜单。状态不再写在标题下方，而是显示在侧面菜单中的下拉菜单中。选民部分已从左侧移至右下角。我现在有三列而不是两列。标题突然变成全宽，并带有不同的菜单项和不同的颜色。<br>6. 我进行更改并想返回查看路线图视图。路线图视图现在看起来也有所不同，因为我处于管理视图中。<br>我认为如果这两个视图合并为一个，将会极大地提高可用性。这可能是一项艰巨的设计挑战，但我认为这会对管理员产生巨大的影响。 | 0 | 0 |
